# Time Period   Productivity                            Value per worker (approx)
# 1700          $ 1.50 - Peasants (x1)                  $ 1.00
# 1800          $ 2.00 - Laborers or higher (x2)        $ 4.00
# 1850          $ 3.00                                  $ 10.00
# 1900          $ 5.00 - Workers or higher (x5)         $ 25.00
# 1950          $ 8.00                                  $ 65.00
# 2000          $ 10.00 - Professionals or higher (x10) $ 100.00
# 2050          $ 12.00 - Specialists only (x20)        $ 240.00

# Time Period   I Prod      II Prod     III Prod    IV Prod     % Input     % Rev
# 1500          $  1.5      $  1.7      $  2.0      $  2.3      20          80
# 1750          $  2.0      $  2.3      $  2.7      $  3.0      25          75
# 1850          $  2.7      $  3.0      $  3.6      $  4.1      30          70
# 1900          $  3.6      $  4.2      $  4.8      $  5.4      35          65
# 1950          $  4.8      $  5.5      $  6.3      $  7.2      40          60
# 2000          $  6.3      $  7.3      $  8.5      $  9.5      45          55
# 2050          $  8.5      $  9.6      $ 11.3      $ 12.8      50          50

# I - Agriculture, Mining, Logging
# II - Consumer Goods, Textiles, Plastics, Chemicals, Urban Center, Entertainment Hub, Early Steel, Synthetic Oil/Rubber/Fiber
# III - Batteries, Tools, Electronics, Appliances, Power Plant, Oil, Late Steel
# IV - Vehicles, Machinery, Computers

# Country Total = Resource Eff. Modifier * ( (Additional Resources + State Production) * Infrastructure Bonus * Local Resources Modifier + Temporary Resources - Resource Cost )
# State resource@token does NOT get modified by modifier@local_resources, but DOES get modified by additional resources & resource cost
# resource@token = (Base + Additional Resources) * Infra - Resource Cost
# Base = (resource@token + Resource Cost) / Infra - Additional Resources

# Infrastructure (Services, small amount of Industrial Cap)
# Railway (Services, Industrial Cap)
# Port (Services, Shipping Cap)

# Subsistence Farm (Mostly Food, small amount of Wood and Fibers)
# Crop Farm (Food)
# Rice Paddy (Food)
# Livestock Ranch (Food, Small amount of Fiber & Luxuries)
# Luxuries Plantation (Luxuries)

# Steel Mill (Steel)
# Machinery Factory (Machinery)
# Chemical Plant (Chemicals)
# Plastics Plant (Plastics)
# Composites Manufactory (Composites)
# Electronics Factory (Electronics)
# Battery Plant (Portable Power Sources)
# Robotics Plant (Robots)

# Consumer Goods Factory (Consumer Goods)
# Textile Mill (Textiles)
# Appliance Factory (Appliances)
# Vehicle Plant (Vehicles)
# Computer Assembly (Computers)
# Power Plant (Electricity)
# Urban Center (Services)
# Entertainment Hub (Entertainment)

# What NEEDS to be displayed:
#

# Note that base employment is determined by BASE OUTPUT * BASE PRICE / 2

# GOVT
    define_pm_industrial_complex = {
        set_variable = { global.pm_construction_duration@token:pm_industrial_complex = 24 }
        clear_array = global.pm_construction_input@token:pm_industrial_complex
        clear_array = global.pm_construction_input_amount@token:pm_industrial_complex
        add_to_array = { global.pm_construction_input@token:pm_industrial_complex = token:wood }
        add_to_array = { global.pm_construction_input_amount@token:pm_industrial_complex = 4.0 }
        add_to_array = { global.pm_construction_input@token:pm_industrial_complex = token:iron }
        add_to_array = { global.pm_construction_input_amount@token:pm_industrial_complex = 4.0 }
        add_to_array = { global.pm_construction_input@token:pm_industrial_complex = token:steel }
        add_to_array = { global.pm_construction_input_amount@token:pm_industrial_complex = 4.0 }
        add_to_array = { global.pm_construction_input@token:pm_industrial_complex = token:machinery }
        add_to_array = { global.pm_construction_input_amount@token:pm_industrial_complex = 4.0 }
        add_to_array = { global.pm_construction_input@token:pm_industrial_complex = token:tools }
        add_to_array = { global.pm_construction_input_amount@token:pm_industrial_complex = 4.0 }

        set_variable = { global.pm_workforce_laborers@token:pm_industrial_complex = 0.9 }
        set_variable = { global.pm_workforce_workers@token:pm_industrial_complex = 0.1 }
    }
